```md
# sig-database
IDA FLIRT Signature Database


### Script
GitHub - push0ebp/ALLirt - [https://github.com/push0ebp/ALLirt](https://github.com/push0ebp/ALLirt)
```

`windows/VC12/VC12.md`:

```md
# VC12 Signatures


### Made on 

OS : Windows 10

IDE : Visual Studio 2013

### File List
```
libcmt.sig 
libcmtd.sig 
msvcrt.sig 
msvcrtd.sig 
msvcprt.sig 
msvcprtd.sig 
```

* libcmt - /MT
* libcmtd - /MTd
* msvc(p)rt - /MD
* msvc(p)rtd - /MDd



I couln't make c++ static library such as libcpmt and libcpmtd.

If you have solution about this problem, contribute this repo or advise me.
```
